# 52. Voice Component Fork Modification Inventory

Generated: 2026-05-18

## Purpose

This document is the public-safe inventory for replaying Viventium voice-component fork changes onto a fresh upstream checkout. It captures the exact delta from each component fork's upstream merge-base to the currently checked Viventium component commit, then turns that delta into a reapply checklist.

Use this before pulling a newer upstream version of a voice component. Do not treat it as a blind patch script: upstream has moved, so every hunk must be reviewed against the new upstream file before it is reapplied.

## Scope

Included upstream fork boundaries:
- `viventium_v0_4/agent-starter-react` (`livekit-examples/agent-starter-react`): modern playground / active browser voice UI.
- `viventium_v0_4/agents-playground` (`livekit/agents-playground`): legacy/classic playground retained as fallback/reference.
- `viventium_v0_4/livekit` (`livekit/livekit`): LiveKit server component fork placeholder; runtime normally uses installed LiveKit server.
- `viventium_v0_4/cartesia-voice-agent` (`livekit-examples/cartesia-voice-agent`): Cartesia example component fork placeholder; active Cartesia route lives in Viventium voice gateway/shared config.

Excluded from this fork-replay inventory:
- `viventium_v0_4/voice-gateway/`: first-party Viventium voice worker code, not a mirrored upstream component repo.
- `viventium_v0_4/LibreChat/`: upstream forked app with voice integration, but not one of the LiveKit/voice component repos named in this inventory. Inventorying LibreChat requires a separate, much larger upstream-delta report.
- `viventium_v0_3_py/interfaces/livekit-playground/`: legacy v0.3 surface, not part of the active v0.4 component set.

## Source-Of-Truth Rules

- The base for each component is `git merge-base HEAD upstream/<branch>` inside that component repo.
- The exact raw line-by-line diffs are generated as a local-only artifact under `tmp/voice-component-fork-inventory/`; keep that artifact out of public commits.
- The hunk-level checklist is the public-safe porting guide for applying equivalent Viventium behavior to a new upstream version.
- Viventium modifications in upstream-derived files should use `VIVENTIUM START` / `VIVENTIUM END` comment wrappers with a short purpose/rationale whenever the file format allows comments.
- Generated lockfiles, binary assets, JSON without comments, and wholesale placeholder deletions cannot always be inline-wrapped; those exceptions must be explained in this inventory and in commits.


## Checklist Legend

- File status codes: `A` = added file, `M` = modified upstream file, `D` = deleted upstream file, and `R###` = renamed file with git similarity percentage.
- Comment audit results: `PASS` means a `VIVENTIUM START` / `VIVENTIUM END` marker pair is present, but the block body still needs a manual description/why/approach review; `REPAIR-TOP` means an added Viventium text file needs a top-of-file block only; `REPAIR-INLINE` means a modified or renamed upstream text file needs inline wrappers around changed Viventium blocks; `REVIEW` means comment support is format-dependent; `COMMENT-LIMITED` means lockfile/generated/JSON-style metadata where wrappers are invalid or undesirable; `N/A` means deletion or binary asset.
- Hunk rows are public-safe location anchors. For exact line-by-line additions/removals, use the ignored raw diff artifact named in the final section.

## High-Level Findings

- `agent-starter-react` is the active modern playground fork. Its Viventium delta contains real product behavior: call-session connection details, explicit LiveKit dispatch, voice route controls, Wing Mode, Listen-Only Mode, transcript stability, recovery/error handling, and branding.
- `agents-playground` is the classic playground fallback/reference. Its Viventium delta keeps explicit-dispatch defaults, audio-first/no-video defaults, local launch helpers, and troubleshooting docs.
- `livekit` is currently a public placeholder component with only a hardened `.gitignore`; the Viventium public-release commit removed upstream server source from the component checkout. Before upgrading this component, decide whether the product still wants a placeholder or a real source-carrying fork.
- `cartesia-voice-agent` is also currently a public placeholder component with only a hardened `.gitignore`; active Cartesia Sonic-3 behavior is implemented elsewhere in Viventium.
- Comment-wrapper compliance is incomplete in the existing voice component forks. Treat every `REPAIR-TOP` and `REPAIR-INLINE` entry below as a required cleanup item while porting to a new upstream base.

### Placeholder Strategy

Current Viventium state keeps this component as a public placeholder: the only source hunk to reapply directly is the hardened `.gitignore`; the rest of the deletion rows record the deliberate upstream-source removal from the public component checkout. On an upstream refresh, decide once whether to retain this placeholder strategy or carry LiveKit server source again. If retaining the placeholder, treat the bulk deletion rows below as evidence of that component-level decision, not independent product-code edits.

### Placeholder Strategy

Current Viventium state keeps this component as a public placeholder: the only source hunk to reapply directly is the hardened `.gitignore`; active Cartesia voice behavior is implemented in the Viventium voice gateway and shared voice contracts. On an upstream refresh, decide once whether to retain the placeholder strategy or carry this example app source again. If retaining the placeholder, treat the bulk deletion rows below as evidence of that component-level decision, not independent product-code edits.

## Porting Procedure Checklist

Use this sequence for each future upstream refresh.

1. [ ] Create a fresh branch from the new upstream component commit.
2. [ ] Replay file-level additions/deletions/renames first, but pause on `livekit` and `cartesia-voice-agent` placeholder deletion decisions.
3. [ ] Replay source hunks one file at a time using the hunk checklist and the local raw diff artifact.
4. [ ] For every touched source/doc file, verify `VIVENTIUM START` / `VIVENTIUM END` wrappers and a short description/why/approach body unless the format forbids comments. Added Viventium files get a top-of-file block; modified upstream files get inline wrappers around changed blocks.
5. [ ] Regenerate lockfiles using the component package manager instead of hand-editing dependency graphs; diff regenerated lockfiles against the prior Viventium lockfiles to confirm required Viventium packages and pins survived.
6. [ ] Run component checks: modern playground `pnpm run lint`, `pnpm exec tsc --noEmit`, `pnpm run build`; classic playground equivalent build/test if retained.
7. [ ] Run parent release checks that cover component pins and voice dispatch contracts.
8. [ ] Run real browser voice QA through the modern playground before claiming the refreshed component works.
9. [ ] Update `components.lock.json` only after nested component commits and built/shipped artifacts match the intended refreshed state.
10. [ ] Run public-safety scans before staging or publishing: no local usernames, home paths, secrets, private URLs, or private runtime artifacts.

## Raw Line-By-Line Diff Handling

The exact raw line-by-line diff for this inventory was generated locally at `tmp/voice-component-fork-inventory/2026-05-18-raw-line-by-line-diffs.md`. That path is intentionally under ignored `tmp/` and must stay out of tracked public docs. The raw appendix includes large deleted upstream source blocks from placeholder component forks, so public release review should rely on the public-safe hunk table above plus locally regenerated raw diffs when doing the actual rebase.

Regenerate the raw diff artifact from the current checked commits with:

```bash
mkdir -p tmp/voice-component-fork-inventory
{
  printf '# Voice Component Fork Raw Line-By-Line Diffs\n\n'
  git -C viventium_v0_4/agent-starter-react diff --binary --find-renames 62c4654086d217bac46f2275c3574840646c6a89..HEAD --src-prefix=upstream/agent-starter-react/ --dst-prefix=viventium/agent-starter-react/
  git -C viventium_v0_4/agents-playground diff --binary --find-renames ee0b50c9f8c6e62fc9710a4d8a8b436ea94c3572..HEAD --src-prefix=upstream/agents-playground/ --dst-prefix=viventium/agents-playground/
  git -C viventium_v0_4/livekit diff --binary --find-renames 9674ac48ab4657796bb5b9bb0e421d5b7723d30e..HEAD --src-prefix=upstream/livekit/ --dst-prefix=viventium/livekit/
  git -C viventium_v0_4/cartesia-voice-agent diff --binary --find-renames 177fa9225ebf8e08fdcd0ab1355a6af270ec359c..HEAD --src-prefix=upstream/cartesia-voice-agent/ --dst-prefix=viventium/cartesia-voice-agent/
} > tmp/voice-component-fork-inventory/2026-05-18-raw-line-by-line-diffs.md
```

Use that local raw file during the future upstream pull/rebase to inspect exact old context and line-by-line additions/removals for each hunk ID. Before any public commit, keep only this tracked inventory unless the raw diff has been separately sanitized and reviewed.
